<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщить.html>приобщи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priobščítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>to accustom, to familiarize <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщать.html>приобща́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знание.html>зна́ниям</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>priobščátʹ</b> k znánijam</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to impart knowledge (to smb)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to join <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщать.html>приобща́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́лу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>priobščátʹ</b> k délu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to file</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">church</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to administer the sacrament <i>(to)</i>, to communicate</li></ol>

***приобщаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приобщаться.html>приобща́ться</a> (31083)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщать.html>приобща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priobščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщаться.html>приобща́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priobščátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщиться.html>приобщи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to join</li>
<li>to become familiar <i>(with)</i>, to familiarize oneself <i>(with)</i>, to learn to use, to enjoy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщаться.html>приобща́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высо́кому</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:искусство.html>иску́сству</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>priobščátʹsja</b> k vysókomu iskússtvu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to enjoy true art</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to communicate</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщать.html>приобща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priobščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщать.html>приобща́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">priobščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщить.html>приобщи́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">priobščítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***приобщить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приобщить.html>приобщи́ть</a> (22443)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-общи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-obščítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщить.html>приобщи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priobščítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщать.html>приобща́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to accustom, to familiarize <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщить.html>приобщи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знание.html>зна́ниям</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>priobščítʹ</b> k znánijam</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to impart knowledge (to smb)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщить.html>приобщи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широ́кие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:масса.html>ма́ссы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:культура.html>культу́ре</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>priobščítʹ</b> širókije mássy k kulʹtúre</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give the masses access to (modern) culture</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to join <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщить.html>приобщи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́лу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>priobščítʹ</b> k délu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to file</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">church</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to administer the sacrament <i>(to)</i>, to communicate</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приостановить.html>приостанови́вший</a> (13475)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приостановить.html>приостанови́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priostanovívšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приостановить.html>приостанови́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priostanovítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приостановиться.html>приостанови́ться</a> (11888)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приостановить.html>приостанови́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priostanovítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***приоткрыть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приоткрыть.html>приоткры́ть</a> (4171)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:открыть.html>откры́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otkrýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приоткрыть.html>приоткры́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priotkrýtʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приоткрывать.html>приоткрыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to open slightly, to set ajar</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">приотвори́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">priotvorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***припадать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:припадать.html>припада́ть</a> (13728)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">припа́д-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pripád-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припадать.html>припада́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pripadátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припасть.html>припа́сть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall down <i>(to)</i>, to press oneself <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:припадать.html>припада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грудь.html>груди</a> кого́-л</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pripadátʹ</b> k grudi kovó-l</i> ― <span class="e-translation">press oneself against smb's breast</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:припадать.html>припада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> чьи́м-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pripadátʹ</b> k čʹím-libo nogám</i> ― <span class="e-translation">prostrate oneself before smb</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:припадать.html>припада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́хом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pripadátʹ</b> úxom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">press one's ear (to)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to limp <i>(slightly)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:припадать.html>припада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вую</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:левый.html>ле́вую</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pripadátʹ</b> na právuju (lévuju) nógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">be lame in the right (left) leg</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***припас.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:припас.html>припа́с</a> (14391)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal noun from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припасти.html>припасти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pripastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припас.html>припа́с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pripás</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припас.html>припа́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припас.html>припа́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припас.html>припа́сов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> supply, provision</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="deprecated-label">plural</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> provisions, victuals</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">припаса́ть</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pripasátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припасти.html>припасти́</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pripastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боеприпас.html>боеприпа́сы</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bojepripásy</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:припасть.html>припа́сть</a> (9679)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pastʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припасть.html>припа́сть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pripástʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припадать.html>припада́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall down <i>(to)</i>, to press oneself <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:припасть.html>припа́сть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грудь.html>груди</a> кого́-л</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pripástʹ</b> k grudi kovó-l</i> ― <span class="e-translation">press oneself against smb's breast</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:припасть.html>припа́сть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> чьи́м-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pripástʹ</b> k čʹím-libo nogám</i> ― <span class="e-translation">prostrate oneself before smb</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:припасть.html>припа́сть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́хом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pripástʹ</b> úxom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">press one's ear (to)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припев.html>припе́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pripév</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припев.html>припе́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припев.html>припе́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припев.html>припе́вов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> refrain, chorus, burden</li></ol>
